                                                                                                                                                                                      A. Interactive Real-World Setup

                                                                                                                                                                                      A. 交互式真实世界设置

                                                                                                                                                                                      In this section, we document the interactive real-world experience with CaP-Agent0 centered around a chat-based web UI, where the user can propose new tasks to the robot, view the step-by-step tool-use results, and offer feedbacks for multi-turn improvement. We will show how this system enables a real-world robot (AgiBot G1) to zero-shot complete novel tasks. 在本节中，我们记录了围绕基于聊天的 Web UI 构建的 CaP-Agent0 交互式真实世界体验。用户可以向机器人提出新任务，查看分步工具使用结果，并提供反馈以进行多轮改进。我们将展示该系统如何使真实世界的机器人（AgiBot G1）能够零样本完成新颖任务。

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.1. User Interface

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.1. 用户界面

                                                                                                                                                                                      On the chat UI shown in Figure 9, the user start with choosing task configurations and models. Then they can view the scene description and code generated by the model. As the code is executed on the robot, they also see the step-by-step progress of each tool call, such as the segmentation masks returned by SAM3, Points annotated by Molmo 2, and wrist camera views when the robot arm moves. In between turns, the user can provide additional feedback to the model by typing in the chatbox on the bottom. 在图 9 所示的聊天界面上，用户首先选择任务配置和模型。随后，他们可以查看场景描述和模型生成的代码。当代码在机器人上执行时，他们还能看到每个工具调用的分步进度，例如 SAM3 返回的分割掩码、Molmo 2 标注的点，以及机器人手臂移动时的腕部摄像头视图。在交互轮次之间，用户可以通过底部的聊天框输入额外反馈来引导模型。

                                                                                                                                                                                      The UI also features a 3D visualization powered by Viser (Yi et al., 2025), which shows the live robot URDF, trajectories, and depth pointcloud. 该界面还具备由 Viser (Yi et al., 2025) 支持的 3D 可视化功能，可显示实时机器人 URDF、轨迹和深度点云。

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.2. Tools

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.2. 工具

                                                                                                                                                                                      CaP-Agent0, specifically on the AgiBot G1, has access to these APIs for perceiving, reasoning, and interacting. CaP-Agent0（特别是在 AgiBot G1 上）可以使用以下 API 进行感知、推理和交互。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • get_observation: returns a dictionary of the current head camera image (RGB, depth, and intrinsics), left and right wrist camera images, end-effector 6-DoF force-wrenches, and joint configuration.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • get_observation：返回一个包含当前头部摄像头图像（RGB、深度和内参）、左右腕部摄像头图像、末端执行器 6 自由度力/力矩以及关节配置的字典。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • segment_sam3_text_prompt: given an image and a text prompt, returns a list of segmentation masks and scores.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • segment_sam3_text_prompt：给定图像和文本提示，返回一组分割掩码和分数。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • segment_sam3_point_prompt: given an image and a point coordinate on the image, returns a list of segmentation masks and scores.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • segment_sam3_point_prompt：给定图像和图像上的点坐标，返回一组分割掩码和分数。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • point_prompt_molmo: given an image and a text prompt, returns a list of points on the image pointed out by Molmo 2.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • point_prompt_molmo：给定图像和文本提示，返回由 Molmo 2 指出的图像点列表。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • open_gripper: opens gripper.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • open_gripper：打开夹爪。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • close_gripper: closes gripper.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • close_gripper：关闭夹爪。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • goto_pose: Plans and executes IK to a pose specified by a position and orientation, optionally with a pre-grasp offset and max force-wrench.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • goto_pose：规划并执行逆运动学（IK）以到达由位置和方向指定的位姿，可选择设置预抓取偏移量和最大力矩。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • matrix_to_pose_wxyz_xyz: Converts a 4×4 transformation matrix to a pose represented in a quaternion and a 3D position.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • matrix_to_pose_wxyz_xyz：将 4×4 变换矩阵转换为由四元数和 3D 位置表示的位姿。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • pose_wxyz_xyz_to_matrix: Converts a pose to a transformation matrix.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • pose_wxyz_xyz_to_matrix：将位姿转换为变换矩阵。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • euler_to_quaternion_wxyz: Converts extrinsic XYZ Euler angles to a quaternion.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • euler_to_quaternion_wxyz：将外在 XYZ 欧拉角转换为四元数。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • quaternion_wxyz_to_euler: Converts quaternion of extrinsic XYZ Euler angles.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • quaternion_wxyz_to_euler：将四元数转换为外在 XYZ 欧拉角。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • query_vlm: Ask a question with text and images to an expert VLM model (Gemini-3-Pro)

                                                                                                                                                                                      • query_vlm：向专家 VLM 模型（Gemini-3-Pro）提出包含文本和图像的问题。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • go_forward: Move forward 1 meter.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • go_forward：向前移动 1 米。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • turn_left_45_degrees: Turn left 45 degrees.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • turn_left_45_degrees：向左转 45 度。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • turn_right_45_degrees: Turn right 45 degrees.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • turn_right_45_degrees：向右转 45 度。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • goto_planar_position: Plan and execute IK to a position with planar motion constraint, but no orientation (yaw) requirement.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • goto_planar_position：规划并执行逆运动学（IK）以到达具有平面运动约束的位置，无需考虑方向（偏航角）。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • convert_depth_to_pointcloud: Given a depth image, intrinsics, and extrinsics, convert the depth image into a pointcloud.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • convert_depth_to_pointcloud：给定深度图像、内参和外参，将深度图像转换为点云。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 9. An example of the web UI, where users can select the task and model at the top, view the model's responses and execution details in the middle, and provide instructions at the bottom. 图 9. Web UI 示例，用户可在顶部选择任务和模型，在中间查看模型的响应和执行详情，并在底部提供指令。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 10. Viser (Yi et al., 2025) visualization section of the web UI. 图 10. Web UI 中的 Viser (Yi et al., 2025) 可视化部分。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 11. An example of CaP-Agent0 locating and grasping an auto pencil refill holder, where it uses Molmo2 to locate the object. 图 11. CaP-Agent0 定位并抓取自动铅笔芯盒的示例，它使用 Molmo2 来定位物体。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • forward_kinematics: Given a robot configuration, compute the end-effector pose.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • forward_kinematics：给定机器人配置，计算末端执行器的位姿。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • overlay_eef_axis_on_image: Visualize end-effector pose on a camera image by rendering the 3D axis on top.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • overlay_eef_axis_on_image：通过在相机图像上叠加渲染 3D 轴，实现末端执行器位姿的可视化。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • overlay_segmentation_masks: Visualize segmentation masks on an image.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • overlay_segmentation_masks：在图像上可视化分割掩码。

                                                                                                                                                                                      • say_something: Convey some intent to the user.

                                                                                                                                                                                      • say_something：向用户传达某种意图。

                                                                                                                                                                                      Among the tools, the 3D rigid body transformation helpers are provided although technically not strictly necessary. We find that when not provided, these functions are almost always written by the models who make mistakes from time to time. 在这些工具中，虽然 3D 刚体变换辅助函数在技术上并非绝对必要，但我们提供了它们。我们发现，如果不提供这些函数，模型几乎总是会自行编写，且偶尔会出错。

                                                                                                                                                                                      Visualization tools such as overlay_eef_axis_on_image and overlay_segmentation_masks enables advanced multi-modal reasoning when the output images are passed to an expert VLM via query_vlm. This allows, for example, code execution conditioning based on if the expert VLM answered "which of these segmentation masks should I pick?". 诸如 overlay_eef_axis_on_image 和 overlay_segmentation_masks 之类的可视化工具，在将输出图像通过 query_vlm 传递给专家 VLM 时，能够实现高级的多模态推理。例如，这允许基于专家 VLM 对“我应该选择这些分割掩码中的哪一个？”的回答来进行代码执行条件判断。

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3. Real World Tasks

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3. 真实世界任务

                                                                                                                                                                                      In this section, we show visualizations of CaP-Agent0 completing tasks in the real world. All experiments are zero-shot. The agent's execution details are condensed and presented as pseudo sub-steps, while CaP-Agent0 writes the underlying code in greater detail using tools available in A.2. Raw code example is available in Appendix E. 在本节中，我们展示了 CaP-Agent0 在真实世界中完成任务的可视化过程。所有实验均为零样本（zero-shot）。智能体的执行细节被浓缩并呈现为伪子步骤，而 CaP-Agent0 则使用 A.2 节中提供的工具编写更详细的底层代码。原始代码示例可在附录 E 中找到。

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3.1. NEEDLE IN A HAYSTACK

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3.1. 大海捞针

                                                                                                                                                                                      In this task, we evaluate the ability of CaP-Agent0 to find "needles in a haystack." Specifically, in a cluttered scene containing diverse objects, the robot is tasked with locating and grasping an auto pencil refill holder, a relatively uncommon item. Such uncommon objects are often challenging for end-to-end learning policies such as VLAs. In contrast, CaP-Agent0 leverages pretrained VLMs to successfully localize and retrieve the target object, as shown in Figure 11. 在此任务中，我们评估 CaP-Agent0“大海捞针”的能力。具体而言，在包含多种物体的杂乱场景中，机器人需要定位并抓取一个相对罕见的物品——自动铅笔芯盒。此类罕见物体对于 VLA 等端到端学习策略来说通常具有挑战性。相比之下，如图 11 所示，CaP-Agent0 利用预训练的 VLM 成功定位并取回了目标物体。

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3.2. MECHANICAL SEARCH

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3.2. 机械搜索

                                                                                                                                                                                      In this task, three inverted cups are placed on a table, and the robot is instructed to retrieve a green lime hidden beneath one of them. This occluded object retrieval problem is commonly referred to as mechanical search (Huang et al., 2022a). Because the lime is concealed by the cups, the robot must systematically explore each cup to locate it. A representative planning and execution example is shown in Figure 12. 在此任务中，桌上放置了三个倒扣的杯子，机器人需取回隐藏在其中一个杯子下的青柠。这种遮挡物体的检索问题通常被称为机械搜索（Huang et al., 2022a）。由于青柠被杯子遮挡，机器人必须系统地探索每个杯子以找到它。图 12 展示了一个典型的规划与执行示例。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 12. Mechanical search planning and execution example. The left column shows the agent planning process and the right column shows the physical robot execution. 图 12. 机械搜索的规划与执行示例。左列显示智能体的规划过程，右列显示物理机器人的执行过程。

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3.3. MULTIMODAL SYMBOLIC REASONING

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3.3. 多模态符号推理

                                                                                                                                                                                      In this task, we evaluate the multimodal symbolic reasoning capabilities of CaP-Agent0 by requiring it to solve a mathematical equation formed by numbered wooden blocks. The robot must first perceive the scene to interpret the equation and then grasp the correct block and place it in correct location to complete the solution, as shown in Figure 13. 在此任务中，我们通过要求 CaP-Agent0 求解由带数字的木块组成的数学等式，来评估其多模态符号推理能力。如图 13 所示，机器人必须首先感知场景以解读等式，然后抓取正确的木块并将其放置在正确位置以完成求解。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 13. Example of a Multimodal Symbolic Reasoning task, where the robot is asked to solve the problem of 59 plus 8. 图 13. 多模态符号推理任务示例，机器人被要求解决 59 加 8 的问题。

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3.4. LEARNING FROM HUMAN FEEDBACK

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3.4. 从人类反馈中学习

                                                                                                                                                                                      CaP-Agent0 is able to incorporate human feedback and adjust its code generation accordingly to complete the task. As shown in Figure 14, the robot is instructed to pick up an apple but fails in the initial attempt due to an excessively high grasp pose. After receiving the feedback "grasped the apple too high," CaP-Agent0 modifies the generated code and successfully completes the task on the second attempt. CaP-Agent0 能够整合人类反馈并相应地调整其代码生成以完成任务。如图 14 所示，机器人被指示拿起一个苹果，但由于抓取姿态过高，首次尝试失败。在收到“抓取苹果的位置太高”的反馈后，CaP-Agent0 修改了生成的代码，并在第二次尝试中成功完成了任务。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 14. Example of picking up an apple. While the first attempt fails, CaP-Agent0 takes human feedback as input, adjusts the code and completes the task successfully. 图 14. 拿起苹果的示例。虽然第一次尝试失败，但 CaP-Agent0 将人类反馈作为输入，调整代码并成功完成了任务。

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3.5. EMBODIED REASONING

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3.5. 具身推理

                                                                                                                                                                                      This task evaluates the embodied reasoning ability of CaP-Agent0, where the robot is asked to "stack objects as high as possible". Because the scene contains both square and round objects, the robot must reason about their physical properties to determine a stable stacking strategy. As shown in Figure 15, CaP-Agent0 learns to place round objects on top of square ones to maximize stability. 此任务评估 CaP-Agent0 的具身推理能力，要求机器人“尽可能高地堆叠物体”。由于场景中同时包含方形和圆形物体，机器人必须推理它们的物理属性以确定稳定的堆叠策略。如图 15 所示，CaP-Agent0 学会了将圆形物体放置在方形物体之上，以实现稳定性最大化。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 15. Example of CaP-Agent0 stacking round objects on top of square objects to form the tallest possible stable stack. 图 15. CaP-Agent0 将圆形物体堆叠在方形物体之上以形成最高稳定堆叠的示例。

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3.6. TOOL GENERALIZATION WITH DOMAIN KNOWLEDGE

                                                                                                                                                                                      A.3.6. 结合领域知识的工具泛化

                                                                                                                                                                                      This task demonstrates the versatility of the code-as-policy interface, where CaP-Agent0 can use tools from arbituary Python packages to assist with the task. We ask the robot to "take the elevator downstairs", which suggests locating and pressing the button, and moving into the elevator. Since the robot is positioned at an angle with respect to the wall, it is not immediately obvious in which direction the button should be pushed. CaP-Agent0 is able to invoke SciPy RANSAC algorithm on the segmented wall pointcloud, and compute the surface normal direction, shown in Figure 16. 此任务展示了“代码即策略”（code-as-policy）接口的多功能性，CaP-Agent0 可调用任意 Python 包中的工具来辅助完成任务。我们要求机器人“乘电梯下楼”，这需要定位并按下按钮，然后进入电梯。由于机器人相对于墙壁呈一定角度，按下按钮的方向并不直观。CaP-Agent0 能够对分割后的墙壁点云调用 SciPy RANSAC 算法，并计算出表面法线方向，如图 16 所示。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 16. Example of robot pushing the elevator button. 图 16. 机器人按下电梯按钮的示例。

                                                                                                                                                                                      C. Additional Takeaways

                                                                                                                                                                                      C. 额外收获

                                                                                                                                                                                      In-Context Examples of API Usage improves performance. In the docstring of each API used in S4, we provided a brief description of the API, the expected datatype, and shape for each input and output. However, due to low code compilation successes from open source models in the initial experiments, we hypothesize that additional prompting may be necessary to increase model performance. Therefore, in addition to the components above, we added API usage examples in the docstring. 上下文中的 API 使用示例可提升性能。在 S4 中使用的每个 API 的文档字符串（docstring）中，我们提供了 API 的简要说明以及每个输入和输出的预期数据类型和形状。然而，由于开源模型在初步实验中的代码编译成功率较低，我们推测可能需要额外的提示来提高模型性能。因此，除上述组件外，我们在文档字符串中增加了 API 使用示例。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 18. Per-model breakdown of usefulness of in-context API Usage 图 18. 上下文中 API 使用示例对各模型的有效性分析

                                                                                                                                                                                      We present the results in Figure 3 and Figure 4, and a per-model breakdown in Figure 18. We observe that almost all models benefited from adding additional context of examples of how to use the low-level APIs. 我们在图 3 和图 4 中展示了结果，并在图 18 中提供了各模型的详细分析。我们观察到，几乎所有模型都受益于添加了如何使用底层 API 的额外上下文示例。

                                                                                                                                                                                      D. Qualitative Analysis of CaP-RL Post-Training Effects

                                                                                                                                                                                      D. CaP-RL 训练后效果的定性分析

                                                                                                                                                                                      In this section, we analyze the qualitative behavioral shifts induced by on-policy reinforcement learning (GRPO) on the Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct base model. We focus on the Stack Red Cube on Green Cube task to illustrate how RL mitigates fundamental instruction-following failures and induces robust geometric reasoning. Methodologically, CaP-RL leverages the privileged S1 tier to stabilize training by removing perception noise. Below we show the code block examples before and after CaP-RL Post-Training. 在本节中，我们分析了策略内强化学习（GRPO）对 Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct 基础模型所引发的定性行为转变。我们重点关注“将红方块堆叠在绿方块上”的任务，以说明强化学习如何缓解基本的指令遵循失败并诱导稳健的几何推理。在方法论上，CaP-RL 利用特权 S1 层通过消除感知噪声来稳定训练。下面我们展示了 CaP-RL 训练前后的代码块示例。

                                                                                                                                                                                      Before CaP-RL Post-Training Model Behavior. Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct base model code generation example on the task Stack Red Cube on Green Cube prior to on-policy reinforcement learning with CaP-RL: CaP-RL 训练前的模型行为。Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct 基础模型在进行 CaP-RL 策略内强化学习前，针对“将红方块堆叠在绿方块上”任务的代码生成示例：

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      import numpy as np import numpy as np

                                                                                                                                                                                      #Get the pose of the green cube #获取绿方块的位姿

                                                                                                                                                                                      green_cube_position, green_cube_quaternion_wxyz, _ = get_object_pose("green cube") green_cube_position, green_cube_quaternion_wxyz, _ = get_object_pose("green cube")

                                                                                                                                                                                      #Calculate the placement position for the red cube #计算红色方块的放置位置

                                                                                                                                                                                      placement_position = np.array(green_cube_position) + np.array([0, 0, 0.05]) # 5 cm placement_position = np.array(green_cube_position) + np.array([0, 0, 0.05]) # 5 厘米

                                                                                                                                                                                          above the green cube     在绿色方块上方

                                                                                                                                                                                      #Move the robot to the placement position #将机器人移动到放置位置

                                                                                                                                                                                      goto_pose(placement_position, (0, 0, 1, 0)), z_approach=0.1) # Use a slight z_approach goto_pose(placement_position, (0, 0, 1, 0)), z_approach=0.1) # 使用微小的 z_approach

                                                                                                                                                                                          for precision     以确保精度

                                                                                                                                                                                      #Open the gripper to release the red cube #打开夹爪以释放红色方块

                                                                                                                                                                                      open_gripper() open_gripper()

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      After CaP-RL Post-Training Model Behavior. Code generation example of Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct model after on-policy reinforcement learning with CaP-RL on the task Stack Red Cube on Green Cube : CaP-RL 后训练模型行为。Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct 模型在通过 CaP-RL 进行策略内强化学习后，针对“将红色方块堆叠在绿色方块上”任务的代码生成示例：

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      import numpy as np import numpy as np

                                                                                                                                                                                      #Get the positions and extents of the red and green cubes #获取红色和绿色方块的位置及范围

                                                                                                                                                                                      red_cube_pos, _, red_cube_extent = get_object_pose("red cube", return_bbox_extent=True) red_cube_pos, _, red_cube_extent = get_object_pose("red cube", return_bbox_extent=True)

                                                                                                                                                                                      green_cube_pos, _, green_cube_extent = get_object_pose("green cube", return_bbox_extent green_cube_pos, _, green_cube_extent = get_object_pose("green cube", return_bbox_extent

                                                                                                                                                                                          =True)     =True)

                                                                                                                                                                                      #Calculate the placement position on top of the green cube #计算绿色方块顶部的放置位置

                                                                                                                                                                                      placement_pos = green_cube_pos + np.array([0, 0, red_cube_extent[2] / 2 + placement_pos = green_cube_pos + np.array([0, 0, red_cube_extent[2] / 2 +

                                                                                                                                                                                          green_cube_extent[2] / 2])     green_cube_extent[2] / 2])

                                                                                                                                                                                      #Sample a grasp pose for the red cube #为红色方块采样抓取位姿

                                                                                                                                                                                      grasp_pos, grasp_quat = sample_grasp_pose("red cube") grasp_pos, grasp_quat = sample_grasp_pose("red cube")

                                                                                                                                                                                      #Move to the grasp pose and approach #移动至抓取位姿并靠近

                                                                                                                                                                                      goto_pose(grasp_pos, grasp_quat, z_approach=0.1) goto_pose(grasp_pos, grasp_quat, z_approach=0.1)

                                                                                                                                                                                      #Close the gripper to grasp the red cube #闭合夹爪以抓取红色方块

                                                                                                                                                                                      close_gripper() close_gripper()

                                                                                                                                                                                      #Move to the placement position #移动至放置位置

                                                                                                                                                                                      goto_pose(placement_pos, (0, 0, 1, 0)), z_approach=0.1) goto_pose(placement_pos, (0, 0, 1, 0)), z_approach=0.1)

                                                                                                                                                                                      #Open the gripper to release the red cube #打开夹爪以释放红色方块

                                                                                                                                                                                      open_gripper() open_gripper()

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Pre-RL Failure Modes: Step Skipping and Hallucinated State. Prior to RL post-training, the base model frequently exhibits "step skipping", a failure mode where the agent attempts to satisfy the final goal state without executing the necessary prerequisites. As shown in the pre-RL snippet, the model correctly identifies the target location (placement_position) but fails to grasp the red cube. It attempts to move the gripper directly to the placement target and open it, seemingly hallucinating that it is already holding the object. RL前失败模式：步骤跳过与状态幻觉。在RL后训练之前，基础模型常表现出“步骤跳过”，即智能体在未执行必要前提条件的情况下试图直接达成最终目标状态。如RL前代码片段所示，模型虽能正确识别目标位置（placement_position），却未能抓取红色方块。它试图直接将夹爪移至放置目标并打开，仿佛产生了已抓取物体的幻觉。

                                                                                                                                                                                      Post-RL Improvement: Causal Sequencing and Geometric Generalization. After GRPO training, two critical improvements emerge: RL后改进：因果序列与几何泛化。经过GRPO训练后，出现了两项关键改进：

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 19. CaP-RL Finetuned Qwen-2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct deployed on the real task put the red cube on the green cube. Human Oracle code gets 21/25 task successes in real. Prior to reinforcement learning, we see behaviors such as grasp approaches on the green cube as the first action, rather than a more sensible approach on the red cube first. 图19。部署于真实任务“将红色方块放置在绿色方块上”的CaP-RL微调版Qwen-2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct。人类专家代码在真实环境中取得21/25的任务成功率。在强化学习之前，我们观察到诸如将“靠近绿色方块”作为首个动作的行为，而非更合理的“先靠近红色方块”。

                                                                                                                                                                                      1. Causal Sequencing: The model correctly synthesizes the full manipulation chain: Identify → Grasp → Transport → Release. It learns through environment interaction and reward feedback signals that the causal dependency that an object must be grasped (via close_gripper) before it can be placed.

                                                                                                                                                                                      2. 因果序列：模型正确合成了完整的操作链：识别 → 抓取 → 搬运 → 释放。它通过环境交互和奖励反馈信号学习到因果依赖关系，即物体必须先被抓取（通过close_gripper）才能被放置。

                                                                                                                                                                                      1. Dynamic Geometric Reasoning: Instead of using hard-coded offsets, the RL-trained model utilizes the return_bbox_extent = True parameter to dynamically calculate the stacking height based on object dimensions (red_extent[2]/2 + green_extent[2]/2). This indicates a shift from memorization to grounded geometric reasoning.

                                                                                                                                                                                      2. 动态几何推理：RL 训练模型不再使用硬编码偏移量，而是利用 return_bbox_extent = True 参数，根据物体尺寸（red_extent[2]/2 + green_extent[2]/2）动态计算堆叠高度。这表明模型已从死记硬背转向基于实体的几何推理。

                                                                                                                                                                                      Zero-shot Generalization to Non-privileged Physical World Setups. Although the model is only post-trained on the privileged S1 tier, the resulting policies demonstrate robust zero-shot transfer to the non-privileged S2 tier. Consequently, the model functions effectively in physical real-world setups, as shown in Figure 19. 对非特权物理世界设置的零样本泛化。尽管模型仅在特权 S1 层级上进行了后训练，但所得策略在非特权 S2 层级上展现出了稳健的零样本迁移能力。因此，如图 19 所示，该模型在物理现实世界设置中也能有效运行。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 20. CaP-RL Finetuned Qwen-2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct successfully deployed on similar task variants. Demonstrates that base model is still capable of instruction following. 图 20. 经 CaP-RL 微调的 Qwen-2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct 成功部署于相似任务变体。证明了基础模型仍具备指令遵循能力。

                                                                                                                                                                                      Zero-Shot Generalization to Task Variants. We observe instruction-following and zero-shot generalization to similar task variants after RL post-training, as seen in 20. The same policy successfully executes variants such as "put the tennis ball on the green cube" or tasks involving randomized object colors, as the underlying logic relies on abstract properties (bounding boxes) rather than overfitting to specific entity names or training instance scales. 对任务变体的零样本泛化。正如 20 所见，在 RL 后训练后，我们观察到了指令遵循和对相似任务变体的零样本泛化能力。同一策略可成功执行诸如“将网球放在绿色方块上”或涉及随机物体颜色的任务，因为其底层逻辑依赖于抽象属性（边界框），而非过拟合于特定的实体名称或训练实例规模。

                                                                                                                                                                                      E. CaP-Agent0 Case Studies

                                                                                                                                                                                      E. CaP-Agent0 案例研究

                                                                                                                                                                                      E.1. Real-World Case Studies

                                                                                                                                                                                      E.1. 现实世界案例研究

                                                                                                                                                                                      E.1.1. COMMON SENSE PHYSICS-AWARE TASK DECOMPOSITION E.1.1. 基于常识物理的复杂任务分解

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 21. "Stack these as high as you can." 图 21. “尽可能高地堆叠这些物体。”

                                                                                                                                                                                      We validate CaP-Agent0 on a real-world Franka Panda platform using a set of geometrically heterogeneous objects: a yellow cube, a blue cube, and a tennis ball. The agent was given the open-ended instruction: "stack these as high as you can." with no additional prompt context outside of API usage documentation and the multimodal agent initial scene description. 我们在 Franka Panda 现实世界平台上验证了 CaP-Agent0，使用了一组几何形状各异的物体：一个黄色方块、一个蓝色方块和一个网球。代理收到的开放式指令为：“尽可能高地堆叠这些物体。”除 API 使用文档和多模态代理初始场景描述外，未提供任何额外的提示上下文。

                                                                                                                                                                                      Crucially, the task prompt provides neither a specific stacking sequence nor any semantic description of the scene or its objects. While a standard visuomotor policy might attempt to stack objects in detection order, potentially attempting to balance a cube on top of the spherical ball, CaP-Agent0 demonstrated common-sense embodied physical reasoning by deriving the only stable construction order. 关键在于，任务提示既未提供具体的堆叠顺序，也未提供场景或物体的任何语义描述。虽然标准的视觉运动策略可能会尝试按检测顺序堆叠物体，甚至可能尝试将方块平衡在球体上方，但 CaP-Agent0 通过推导出唯一稳定的构建顺序，展现了基于常识的具身物理推理能力。

                                                                                                                                                                                      This behavior is enabled by the CaP-Agent0 auxiliary VDM multimodal agent that extracts task-relevant image information before code generation begins. Prompted to "describe the initial state of the environment with the goal of the task in mind," the VLM emits the following context for the coding agent's initial turn: 这种行为得益于 CaP-Agent0 的辅助 VDM 多模态代理，它在代码生成开始前提取了与任务相关的图像信息。在被提示“结合任务目标描述环境的初始状态”时，VLM 为编码代理的初始轮次输出了以下上下文：

                                                                                                                                                                                      "...The cubes appear to have flat surfaces suitable for stacking, while the tennis ball is spherical and would likely need to be placed on top or handled carefully." “……方块表面平坦，适合堆叠，而网球呈球形，可能需要放置在最上方或小心处理。”

                                                                                                                                                                                      Leveraging this textual grounding, the coding agent explicitly decomposed the problem based on stability constraints. The full code generated by the CaP-Agent0 agent for completing this task is found in Appendix H.1. 利用这种文本基础，编码代理明确地基于稳定性约束分解了问题。CaP-Agent0 完成此任务生成的完整代码见附录 H.1。

                                                                                                                                                                                      E.1.2. IMPLICIT MULTI-STEP REASONING FOR OBSTRUCTED GOALS E.1.2. 针对受阻目标的隐式多步推理

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 22. "Place the blue cube on top of the yellow cube." 图 22. “将蓝色方块放在黄色方块上方。”

                                                                                                                                                                                      We evaluate CaP-Agent0 on a task where the Franka Panda must place a blue cube on top of a yellow cube. In the initial state, the cubes form a three-object tower: blue is at the base, supporting yellow, which in turn supports a green cube (Figure 22). 我们评估了 CaP-Agent0 在 Franka Panda 必须将蓝色方块放置在黄色方块之上的任务中的表现。在初始状态下，这些方块构成了一个三层塔：蓝色方块位于底部，支撑着黄色方块，黄色方块上方又支撑着一个绿色方块（图 22）。

                                                                                                                                                                                      The goal prompt "place the blue cube on top of the yellow cube" is linguistically underspecified; it contains no mention of the green obstruction nor the fact that the blue target currently supports the yellow destination. 提示词“将蓝色方块放置在黄色方块上方”在语言上描述不足；它既未提及绿色障碍物，也未说明蓝色目标方块当前正支撑着黄色目标方块这一事实。

                                                                                                                                                                                      CaP-Agent0 resolves this dependency through its auxiliary multimodal perception layer. Before code generation, the VLM provides the coding agent with a high-level strategic prior: CaP-Agent0 通过其辅助多模态感知层解决了这一依赖问题。在生成代码之前，VLM 为编码智能体提供了高层级的策略先验：

                                                                                                                                                                                      "...the blue cube is at the bottom of the stack, underneath the yellow cube, and the yellow cube is underneath a green cube. This implies a complex manipulation task where the robot will likely need to: 1. Remove the top (green) cube. 2. Remove the middle (yellow) cube to access the blue one, or move the stack. 3. Ultimately re-arrange them such that the blue cube ends up on top of the yellow one. The straightforward description is that the target blue cube is currently obstructed and supporting the target destination object (the yellow cube)." “……蓝色方块位于堆叠的最底部，在黄色方块下方，而黄色方块又位于绿色方块下方。这意味着一项复杂的操纵任务，机器人很可能需要：1. 移除顶部的（绿色）方块。2. 移除中间的（黄色）方块以接触蓝色方块，或者移动整个堆叠。3. 最终重新排列它们，使得蓝色方块位于黄色方块之上。直观的描述是，目标蓝色方块目前被遮挡，且支撑着目标目的地物体（黄色方块）。”

                                                                                                                                                                                      This behavior demonstrates that programmatic agents, when augmented with a dedicated perception-to-text grounding layer, can derive complex manipulation strategies traditionally requiring extensive task-specific imitation learning data or manual state-machine design. The full executable rollout is provided in Appendix H.2. 这种行为表明，当程序化智能体配备了专门的感知到文本的接地层（grounding layer）时，能够推导出复杂的操纵策略，而这些策略传统上需要大量的特定任务模仿学习数据或手动设计状态机。完整的可执行过程见附录 H.2。

                                                                                                                                                                                      E.2. Simulation Case Studies

                                                                                                                                                                                      E.2. 仿真案例研究

                                                                                                                                                                                      E.2.1. VERIFICATION AND RETRY BEHAVIOR ENABLED BY MULTITURN DESIGN

                                                                                                                                                                                      E.2.1. 多轮设计实现的验证与重试行为

                                                                                                                                                                                      This case study comes from the "pick up the red cube" task from Robosuite ported into CaP-Gym. Unlike one-shot code generation frameworks, the multi-turn architecture of CaP-Agent0 allows for emergent agentic resilience. In several simulation trials, we observed instances where a planned grasp was physically executed but failed to successfully lift the object due to physics-engine stochasticity or sub-optimal contact points. Rather than terminating the task upon failure, the agent utilized the subsequent turn's observation to verify that the goal condition (e.g., z object >z table  ) remained unfulfilled. As shown in the generated logic, the agent autonomously synthesized a recovery routine branch. This capacity to reason about execution failures and reset the environment state demonstrates that CaP-Agent0 can function as a closed-loop reactive agent rather than a static script generator. 本案例研究源自 Robosuite 中移植到 CaP-Gym 的“拾取红色方块”任务。与一次性代码生成框架不同，CaP-Agent0 的多轮架构实现了涌现式的智能体韧性。在多次仿真试验中，我们观察到一些实例：规划的抓取动作虽已物理执行，但由于物理引擎的随机性或接触点不理想，未能成功提起物体。智能体并未在失败时终止任务，而是利用后续轮次的观测来验证目标条件（例如 z object >z table  ）是否仍未满足。如生成的逻辑所示，智能体自主合成了恢复例程分支。这种针对执行失败进行推理并重置环境状态的能力，证明了 CaP-Agent0 可以作为闭环反应式智能体运行，而非仅仅是一个静态脚本生成器。

                                                                                                                                                                                      E.2.2. PERCEPTION MODULE CASCADE FAILURE FALLBACKS

                                                                                                                                                                                      E.2.2. 感知模块级联故障的回退机制

                                                                                                                                                                                      This case study comes from the "wipe up the brown spill" task from Robosuite ported into CaP-Gym. The model frequently constructs robust perception pipelines that utilize hierarchical fallbacks. It understands that a generic text prompt might fail or be imprecise. In several trials, the model employs a VLM (Molmo) to visually ground the target ("brown spill") into a specific 2D point, and then uses that point to prompt a segmentation model (SAM3) for a precise mask. If this high-precision 本案例研究源自 Robosuite 中移植到 CaP-Gym 的“擦除棕色污渍”任务。模型经常构建出利用分层回退机制的稳健感知流水线。它理解通用的文本提示可能会失败或不够精确。在多次试验中，模型采用 VLM (Molmo) 将目标（“棕色污渍”）在视觉上定位为特定的二维点，然后利用该点提示分割模型 (SAM3) 获取精确掩码。如果这种高精度

                                                                                                                                                                                      method fails, it falls back to broader text prompts like "stain" or "brown object". 方法失败，它会回退到更宽泛的文本提示，如“污渍”或“棕色物体”。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      ...

                                                                                                                                                                                      E.2.3. Geometric Reasoning for Grasp Selection

                                                                                                                                                                                      E.2.3. 抓取选择的几何推理

                                                                                                                                                                                      This case study illustrates how CaP-Agent0 enhances sub-symbolic planners by injecting context-aware strategy. While modules like Contact-GraspNet infer many 6D grasp poses along with confidence scores, the learned scoring lacks awareness of the broader task setting. For this tabletop scenario, the agent correctly identified that a top-down approach strategy is inherently more reliable than side-approaches, regardless of their raw grasp scores. 本案例研究展示了 CaP-Agent0 如何通过注入情境感知策略来增强次符号规划器。虽然 Contact-GraspNet 等模块能推断出许多带有置信度分数的 6D 抓取姿态，但学习到的评分缺乏对更广泛任务环境的感知。对于此桌面场景，智能体正确识别出，无论原始抓取分数如何，自上而下的接近策略本质上都比侧向接近更可靠。

                                                                                                                                                                                      To enforce this strategy, the agent autonomously synthesized a geometric constraint wrapper. By computing the alignment between grasp approach vectors and the world vertical, the generated code filtered out high-scoring but suboptimal side-grasps, explicitly selecting a vertical candidate to maximize stability. The agent also synthesized an autonomous fallback branch: if this strict strategy yielded no candidates, the logic reverted to the global maximum score to prevent execution stagnation. This demonstrates the agent's capacity to wrap generic tools in context-specific logic, bridging the gap between raw geometric perception and high-level task semantics. 为了执行该策略，智能体自主合成了一个几何约束包装器。通过计算抓取接近向量与世界垂直方向的对齐度，生成的代码过滤掉了分数虽高但次优的侧向抓取，明确选择了垂直候选方案以最大化稳定性。智能体还合成了一个自主回退分支：如果这一严格策略未产生候选方案，逻辑将恢复为全局最高分，以防止执行停滞。这证明了智能体能够将通用工具封装在特定情境的逻辑中，弥合了原始几何感知与高层任务语义之间的鸿沟。

                                                                                                                                                                                      Crucially, the automatically synthesized skill library (Appendix G.1) contains an analogous grasp filter, serving as a primary example of the agent's capacity to synthesize task-agnostic geometric logic into its persistent codebase. 至关重要的是，自动合成的技能库（附录 G.1）包含一个类似的抓取过滤器，这是智能体将其任务无关的几何逻辑合成到其持久代码库中能力的典型范例。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      ...

                                                                                                                                                                                      Notice how there is no fallback for the sample_grasp_pose () generation. When the initial code was executed, the outputted grasp was invalid. The model reasoned that the grasp was invalid because it was too close to the origin, so in the subsequent generation, the model retroactively implemented a fallback which only prevents the failure case it just encountered. 请注意，sample_grasp_pose () 的生成过程缺乏回退机制。当初始代码执行时，输出的抓取点无效。模型推断该抓取点无效是因为其过于靠近原点，因此在后续生成中，模型追溯性地实现了一个仅能防止其刚遇到的故障情况的回退方案。

                                                                                                                                                                                      F. Low-Level Perception and Control Primitives

                                                                                                                                                                                      F. 底层感知与控制原语

                                                                                                                                                                                      This section provides the complete specifications for the low-level perception and control primitives used in CaP-Bench, including function signatures, interface definitions, and documentation strings. These primitives constitute the exact specifications provided to agents in Tier S3. Tier S4 utilizes an identical primitive set, but with in-context usage examples (the Example: sections within docstrings) stripped. Tiers S1 and S2 operate on high-level abstractions that are constructed by composing these fundamental primitives. 本节提供了CaP-Bench所用底层感知与控制原语的完整规范，包括函数签名、接口定义及文档字符串。这些原语构成了提供给S3层智能体的确切规范。S4层使用相同的原语集，但去除了上下文中的使用示例（即文档字符串中的“示例：”部分）。S1和S2层则基于由这些基础原语组合而成的高级抽象进行操作。

                                                                                                                                                                                                  prev_cfg=prev_cfg,             prev_cfg=prev_cfg,

                                                                                                                                                                                              )

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                              if prev_cfg is not None:         if prev_cfg is not None:

                                                                                                                                                                                                      break                 break

                                                                                                                                                                                                  else:             else:

                                                                                                                                                                                          joints = np.asarray(self.cfg[:-1], dtype=np.float64).reshape(7)     joints = np.asarray(self.cfg[:-1], dtype=np.float64).reshape(7)
