                                                                                                                                                                                      def rotation_matrix_to_quaternion(R: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray: def rotation_matrix_to_quaternion(R: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:

                                                                                                                                                                                          Convert a 3x3 rotation matrix to a unit quaternion [w,x,y,z] .     将 3x3 旋转矩阵转换为单位四元数 [w,x,y,z] 。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Implements the robust Sheppard's method (checking trace and diagonal elements)     实现稳健的谢泼德（Sheppard）方法（检查迹和对角元素）

                                                                                                                                                                                          to avoid numerical instability when the trace is close to zero.     以避免迹接近零时的数值不稳定。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Args:     参数：

                                                                                                                                                                                              R: (3, 3) rotation matrix.         R: (3, 3) 旋转矩阵。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Returns:     返回：

                                                                                                                                                                                              np.array: [w, x, y, z] unit quaternion.         np.array: [w, x, y, z] 单位四元数。

                                                                                                                                                                                          """

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          tr = np.trace(R)     tr = np.trace(R)

                                                                                                                                                                                          if tr > 0:     if tr > 0:

                                                                                                                                                                                              S = np.sqrt(tr + 1.0) * 2         S = np.sqrt(tr + 1.0) * 2

                                                                                                                                                                                              w = 0.25 * S

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                              x = (R[2, 1] - R[1, 2]) / S         x = (R[2, 1] - R[1, 2]) / S

                                                                                                                                                                                              y = (R[0, 2] - R[2, 0]) / S         y = (R[0, 2] - R[2, 0]) / S

                                                                                                                                                                                              z = (R[1, 0] - R[0, 1]) / S         z = (R[1, 0] - R[0, 1]) / S

                                                                                                                                                                                          elif (R[0, 0] > R[1, 1]) and (R[0, 0] > R[2, 2]):     elif (R[0, 0] > R[1, 1]) and (R[0, 0] > R[2, 2]):

                                                                                                                                                                                              S = np.sqrt(1.0 + R[0, 0] - R[1, 1] - R[2, 2]) * 2         S = np.sqrt(1.0 + R[0, 0] - R[1, 1] - R[2, 2]) * 2

                                                                                                                                                                                              w = (R[2, 1] - R[1, 2]) / S         w = (R[2, 1] - R[1, 2]) / S

                                                                                                                                                                                              x = 0.25 * S

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                              y = (R[0, 1] + R[1, 0]) / S         y = (R[0, 1] + R[1, 0]) / S

                                                                                                                                                                                              z = (R[0, 2] + R[2, 0]) / S         z = (R[0, 2] + R[2, 0]) / S

                                                                                                                                                                                          elif R[1, 1] > R[2, 2]:     elif R[1, 1] > R[2, 2]:

                                                                                                                                                                                              S = np.sqrt(1.0 + R[1, 1] - R[0, 0] - R[2, 2]) * 2         S = np.sqrt(1.0 + R[1, 1] - R[0, 0] - R[2, 2]) * 2

                                                                                                                                                                                              w = (R[0, 2] - R[2, 0]) / S         w = (R[0, 2] - R[2, 0]) / S

                                                                                                                                                                                              x = (R[0, 1] + R[1, 0]) / S         x = (R[0, 1] + R[1, 0]) / S

                                                                                                                                                                                              y = 0.25 * S

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                              z―=(R[1,2]+R[2,1])/s

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          else:     else:

                                                                                                                                                                                              S = np.sqrt(1.0 + R[2,2] - R[0,0] - R[1,1]) * 2         S = np.sqrt(1.0 + R[2,2] - R[0,0] - R[1,1]) * 2

                                                                                                                                                                                              w = (R[1, 0] - R[0, 1]) / S         w = (R[1, 0] - R[0, 1]) / S

                                                                                                                                                                                              x = (R[0, 2] + R[2, 0]) / S         x = (R[0, 2] + R[2, 0]) / S

                                                                                                                                                                                              y = (R[1, 2] + R[2, 1]) / S         y = (R[1, 2] + R[2, 1]) / S

                                                                                                                                                                                              z = 0.25 * S

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          return np.array([w, x, y, z])     return np.array([w, x, y, z])

                                                                                                                                                                                      def decompose_transform(T: np.ndarray) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]: def decompose_transform(T: np.ndarray) -> tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:

                                                                                                                                                                                          Decompose a 4x4 homogeneous transformation matrix into position and quaternion.     将4x4齐次变换矩阵分解为位置和四元数。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Args:     参数：

                                                                                                                                                                                              T: (4, 4) homogeneous transformation matrix.         T: (4, 4) 齐次变换矩阵。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Returns:     返回：

                                                                                                                                                                                              tuple:         元组：

                                                                                                                                                                                                  - position: (3, np.array             - position: (3,) np.array

                                                                                                                                                                                          """

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                                  - quaternion: (4,) np.array [w, x, y, z]             - quaternion: (4,) np.array [w, x, y, z]

                                                                                                                                                                                          position =T[:3,3]     position =T[:3,3]

                                                                                                                                                                                          R = T[:3, :3]

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          quat = rotation_matrix_to_quaternion(R)     quat = rotation_matrix_to_quaternion(R)

                                                                                                                                                                                          return position, quat     return position, quat

                                                                                                                                                                                      def depth_to_point_cloud(depth_img: np.ndarray, intrinsics: np.ndarray) -> np. def depth_to_point_cloud(depth_img: np.ndarray, intrinsics: np.ndarray) -> np.

                                                                                                                                                                                      ndarray: ndarray:

                                                                                                                                                                                          """

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          Convert a depth image to a 3D point cloud in the Camera Frame.     将深度图像转换为相机坐标系下的3D点云。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Args:     参数：

                                                                                                                                                                                              depth img: (H, W) depth map in meters.         depth img: (H, W) 米为单位的深度图。

                                                                                                                                                                                              intrinsics: (3, 3) camera intrinsic matrix.         intrinsics: (3, 3) 相机内参矩阵。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Returns:     返回：

                                                                                                                                                                                              np.array: (H, W, 3) image of 3D coordinates.         np.array: (H, W, 3) 3D 坐标图像。

                                                                                                                                                                                          """

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          if depth_img.ndim == 3:     if depth_img.ndim == 3:

                                                                                                                                                                                              depth_img = depth_img[:, :, 0]         depth_img = depth_img[:, :, 0]

                                                                                                                                                                                          h, w = depth_img.shape     h, w = depth_img.shape

                                                                                                                                                                                          fx = intrinsics[0, 0]     fx = intrinsics[0, 0]

                                                                                                                                                                                          fy = intrinsics[1, 1]     fy = intrinsics[1, 1]

                                                                                                                                                                                          cx = intrinsics[0, 2]     cx = intrinsics[0, 2]

                                                                                                                                                                                          cy = intrinsics[1, 2]     cy = intrinsics[1, 2]

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Vectorized grid generation     #向量化网格生成

                                                                                                                                                                                          y_grid, x_grid = np.mgrid[0:h, 0:w]     y_grid, x_grid = np.mgrid[0:h, 0:w]

                                                                                                                                                                                          z = depth_img     z = depth_img

                                                                                                                                                                                          x=(x− grid - cx )∗z/fx

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          y=(y_ grid - cy )∗z/fy

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          return np.dstack((x, y, z))     return np.dstack((x, y, z))

                                                                                                                                                                                      def mask_to_world_points( ) def mask_to_world_points( )

                                                                                                                                                                                          mask: np.ndarray, depth: np.ndarray, intrinsics: np.ndarray, extrinsics: np.     mask: np.ndarray, depth: np.ndarray, intrinsics: np.ndarray, extrinsics: np.

                                                                                                                                                                                      ndarray ndarray

                                                                                                                                                                                      ) -> np.ndarray: ) -> np.ndarray:

                                                                                                                                                                                          Convert specific pixels defined by a binary mask into 3D points in the World     将由二值掩码定义的特定像素转换为世界坐标系下的3D点。

                                                                                                                                                                                      Frame. Frame.

                                                                                                                                                                                          Args:     参数：

                                                                                                                                                                                              mask: (H, W) binary mask (0 or 1).         mask: (H, W) 二值掩码（0或1）。

                                                                                                                                                                                              depth: (H, W) depth map.         depth: (H, W) 深度图。

                                                                                                                                                                                              intrinsics: (3, 3) camera intrinsics.         intrinsics: (3, 3) 相机内参。

                                                                                                                                                                                              extrinsics: (4, 4) camera-to-world pose matrix.         extrinsics: (4, 4) 相机到世界的位姿矩阵。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Returns:     返回：

                                                                                                                                                                                              np.array: (N, 3) array of valid 3D points in world coordinates.         np.array: (N, 3) 世界坐标系下的有效3D点数组。

                                                                                                                                                                                          """

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Get pixel coordinates     #获取像素坐标

                                                                                                                                                                                          ys, xs = np.where(mask > 0)     ys, xs = np.where(mask > 0)

                                                                                                                                                                                          if len(ys) == 0:     if len(ys) == 0:

                                                                                                                                                                                              return np.empty((0, 3))         return np.empty((0, 3))

                                                                                                                                                                                          z_vals = depth[ys, xs]     z_vals = depth[ys, xs]

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Filter invalid depth     #过滤无效深度

                                                                                                                                                                                          valid =z _vals >0     valid =z _vals >0

                                                                                                                                                                                          ys = ys[valid]     ys = ys[valid]

                                                                                                                                                                                          xs = xs[valid]     xs = xs[valid]

                                                                                                                                                                                          z = z_vals[valid]     z = z_vals[valid]

                                                                                                                                                                                          fx = intrinsics[0, 0]     fx = intrinsics[0, 0]

                                                                                                                                                                                          fy = intrinsics[1, 1]     fy = intrinsics[1, 1]

                                                                                                                                                                                          cx = intrinsics[0, 2]     cx = intrinsics[0, 2]

                                                                                                                                                                                          cy = intrinsics[1, 2]     cy = intrinsics[1, 2]

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Deproject to Camera Frame     #反投影至相机坐标系

                                                                                                                                                                                          x_cam = (xs - cx) * z / fx     x_cam = (xs - cx) * z / fx

                                                                                                                                                                                          y_cam = (ys - cy) * z / fy     y_cam = (ys - cy) * z / fy

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Stack to (N, 3)     #堆叠为 (N, 3)

                                                                                                                                                                                          points_cam = np.stack([x_cam, y_cam, z], axis=-1)     points_cam = np.stack([x_cam, y_cam, z], axis=-1)

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Transform to World Frame     #转换至世界坐标系

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Create homogeneous coordinates (N, 4)     #创建齐次坐标 (N, 4)

                                                                                                                                                                                          points_cam_hom = np.hstack([points_cam, np.ones((len(points_cam), 1)))     points_cam_hom = np.hstack([points_cam, np.ones((len(points_cam), 1)))

                                                                                                                                                                                          points_world_hom = (extrinsics @ points_cam_hom.T). T     points_world_hom = (extrinsics @ points_cam_hom.T). T

                                                                                                                                                                                          return points_world_hom[:, :3]     return points_world_hom[:, :3]

                                                                                                                                                                                      def pixel_to_world_point( ) def pixel_to_world_point( )

                                                                                                                                                                                          u: int, v: int, z: float, intrinsics: np.ndarray, extrinsics: np.ndarray     u: int, v: int, z: float, intrinsics: np.ndarray, extrinsics: np.ndarray

                                                                                                                                                                                      ) -> np.ndarray: ) -> np.ndarray:

                                                                                                                                                                                          Deproject a single pixel to a 3D world point.     将单个像素反投影为三维世界坐标点。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Args:     参数：

                                                                                                                                                                                              u, v: Pixel coordinates (col, row).         u, v: 像素坐标（列，行）。

                                                                                                                                                                                              z: Depth at that pixel.         z: 该像素处的深度。

                                                                                                                                                                                              intrinsics: (3, 3) matrix.         intrinsics: (3, 3) 矩阵。

                                                                                                                                                                                              extrinsics: (4, 4) matrix.         extrinsics: (4, 4) 矩阵。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Returns:     返回：

                                                                                                                                                                                              np.array: [x, y, z] in world frame.         np.array: 世界坐标系下的 [x, y, z]。

                                                                                                                                                                                          """

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          fx = intrinsics[0, 0]     fx = intrinsics[0, 0]

                                                                                                                                                                                          fy = intrinsics[1, 1]     fy = intrinsics[1, 1]

                                                                                                                                                                                          CX = intrinsics[0, 2]     CX = intrinsics[0, 2]

                                                                                                                                                                                          cy = intrinsics[1, 2]     cy = intrinsics[1, 2]

                                                                                                                                                                                          x_cam = (u - cx) * z / fx     x_cam = (u - cx) * z / fx

                                                                                                                                                                                          Y_cam = (v - cy) * z / fy     Y_cam = (v - cy) * z / fy

                                                                                                                                                                                          p_cam = np.array([x_cam, y_cam, z, 1.0])     p_cam = np.array([x_cam, y_cam, z, 1.0])

                                                                                                                                                                                          p_world = extrinsics @ p_cam     p_world = extrinsics @ p_cam

                                                                                                                                                                                          return p_world[:3]     return p_world[:3]

                                                                                                                                                                                      def transform_points(points: np.ndarray, transform_matrix: np.ndarray) -> np. def transform_points(points: np.ndarray, transform_matrix: np.ndarray) -> np.

                                                                                                                                                                                      ndarray: ndarray:

                                                                                                                                                                                          """

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          Apply a 4x4 homogeneous transform to a set of 3D points.     对一组三维点应用 4x4 齐次变换。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Args:     参数：

                                                                                                                                                                                              points: (N, 3) or (H, W, 3) array of points.         points: (N, 3) 或 (H, W, 3) 的点数组。

                                                                                                                                                                                              transform matrix: (4, 4) homogeneous transformation matrix.         transform matrix: (4, 4) 齐次变换矩阵。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Returns:     返回：

                                                                                                                                                                                              np.array: Transformed points with same shape as input.         np.array: 与输入形状相同的变换后点集。

                                                                                                                                                                                          1111

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          original_shape = points.shape     original_shape = points.shape

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Flatten to (N, 3)     #展平为 (N, 3)

                                                                                                                                                                                          points_reshaped = points.reshape(-1, 3)     points_reshaped = points.reshape(-1, 3)

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Convert to homogeneous (N, 4)     #转换为齐次坐标 (N, 4)

                                                                                                                                                                                          ones = np.ones((points_reshaped.shape[0], 1))     ones = np.ones((points_reshaped.shape[0], 1))

                                                                                                                                                                                          points_hom = np.hstack((points_reshaped, ones))     points_hom = np.hstack((points_reshaped, ones))

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Apply transform: (4,4) @ (4,N)→(4,N)→ Transpose back to (N,4)     #应用变换：(4,4) @ (4,N)→(4,N)→ 转置回 (N,4)

                                                                                                                                                                                          points_transformed = (transform_matrix @ points_hom.T).T     points_transformed = (transform_matrix @ points_hom.T).T

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Return to (N, 3) and original shape     #恢复为 (N, 3) 及原始形状

                                                                                                                                                                                          return points_transformed[:, :3].reshape(original_shape)     return points_transformed[:, :3].reshape(original_shape)

                                                                                                                                                                                      def interpolate_segment( ) def interpolate_segment( )

                                                                                                                                                                                          p1: np.ndarray, p2: np.ndarray, step: float = 0.03     p1: np.ndarray, p2: np.ndarray, step: float = 0.03

                                                                                                                                                                                      ) -> list[np.ndarray]: ) -> list[np.ndarray]:

                                                                                                                                                                                          """

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          Generate waypoints along a line segment between two 3D points.     生成两点间线段上的路径点。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Args:     参数：

                                                                                                                                                                                              pl: Start point (3,).         pl: 起点 (3,)。

                                                                                                                                                                                              p2: End point (3,).         p2: 终点 (3,)。

                                                                                                                                                                                              step: Distance between waypoints in meters.         step: 航点间距离（米）。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Returns:     返回：

                                                                                                                                                                                              list[np.ndarray]: List of points including p1 and p2.         list[np.ndarray]: 包含 p1 和 p2 的点列表。

                                                                                                                                                                                          """

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          dist = np.linalg.norm(p2 - p1)     dist = np.linalg.norm(p2 - p1)

                                                                                                                                                                                          if dist < 1e-6:     if dist < 1e-6:

                                                                                                                                                                                              return [p1]         return [p1]

                                                                                                                                                                                          num_points = int(np.ceil(dist / step))     num_points = int(np.ceil(dist / step))

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Using linspace to ensure we hit the start and end exactly     #使用 linspace 确保精确到达起点和终点

                                                                                                                                                                                          return [p1 + (p2 - p1) * t for t in np.linspace(0, 1, num_points + 1)]     return [p1 + (p2 - p1) * t for t in np.linspace(0, 1, num_points + 1)]

                                                                                                                                                                                      def normalize_vector(v: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray: def normalize_vector(v: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:

                                                                                                                                                                                          || || ||

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          Normalize a vector to unit length.     将向量归一化为单位长度。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Args:     参数：

                                                                                                                                                                                              v: (3, ) vector.         v: (3, ) 向量。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Returns:     返回：

                                                                                                                                                                                              np.array: (3, ) unit vector.         np.array: (3, ) 单位向量。

                                                                                                                                                                                          nun     空

                                                                                                                                                                                          norm = np.linalg.norm(v)     norm = np.linalg.norm(v)

                                                                                                                                                                                          if norm < 1e-6:     if norm < 1e-6:

                                                                                                                                                                                              return v / norm         return v / norm

                                                                                                                                                                                          return v / norm     return v / norm

                                                                                                                                                                                      def select_top_down_grasp( ) def select_top_down_grasp( )

                                                                                                                                                                                          grasps: np.ndarray,     grasps: np.ndarray,

                                                                                                                                                                                          scores: np.ndarray,     scores: np.ndarray,

                                                                                                                                                                                          cam_to_world: np.ndarray,     cam_to_world: np.ndarray,

                                                                                                                                                                                          vertical_threshold: float = 0.8,     vertical_threshold: float = 0.8,

                                                                                                                                                                                      ) -> tuple: ) -> tuple:

                                                                                                                                                                                          1111

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          Selects the best grasp that aligns the gripper vertically (Top-Down).     选择垂直对齐夹爪的最佳抓取方式（自上而下）。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Args:     参数：

                                                                                                                                                                                              grasps: (N, 4, 4) Grasp poses in camera frame.         grasps: (N, 4, 4) 相机坐标系下的抓取位姿。

                                                                                                                                                                                              scores: (N, ) Grasp scores.         scores: (N, ) 抓取评分。

                                                                                                                                                                                              cam_to_world: (4, 4) Extrinsics matrix.         cam_to_world: (4, 4) 外参矩阵。

                                                                                                                                                                                              vertical_threshold: Dot product threshold (1.0 is perfectly vertical).         vertical_threshold: 点积阈值（1.0 为完全垂直）。

                                                                                                                                                                                          Returns:     返回：

                                                                                                                                                                                              tuple: (best_grasp_world_matrix, best_score) or (None, -inf)         tuple: (best_grasp_world_matrix, best_score) 或 (None, -inf)

                                                                                                                                                                                          """

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          best_grasp = None     best_grasp = None

                                                                                                                                                                                          best_score = -np.float64("inf")     best_score = -np.float64("inf")

                                                                                                                                                                                          #World Z axis (vertical)     #世界坐标系 Z 轴（垂直）

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          world_z = np.array([0, 0, 1])     world_z = np.array([0, 0, 1])

                                                                                                                                                                                          for i, g_camera in enumerate(grasps):     for i, g_camera in enumerate(grasps):

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Transform grasp to world frame         #将抓取位姿转换至世界坐标系

                                                                                                                                                                                              g_world = cam_to_world @ g_camera         g_world = cam_to_world @ g_camera

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Extract rotation         #提取旋转矩阵

                                                                                                                                                                                              R = g_world[:3, :3]         R = g_world[:3, :3]

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Assuming Gripper Z or Y is the approach vector depending on gripper         #假设夹爪的 Z 轴或 Y 轴为接近向量，具体取决于夹爪

                                                                                                                                                                                      definition. 定义。

                                                                                                                                                                                              #For Franka/Robotiq, the approach vector is usually the Z-axis of the end         #对于 Franka/Robotiq，接近向量通常是末端执行器的

                                                                                                                                                                                      effector. Z 轴。

                                                                                                                                                                                              gripper_approach =R[:,2]         机械爪接近 =R[:,2]

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Check alignment with negative World Z (pointing down)         #检查与世界坐标系负Z轴（向下）的对齐情况

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Dot product should be close to -1 for top-down         #对于自上而下的抓取，点积应接近 -1

                                                                                                                                                                                              alignment = -np.dot (gripper_approach,world_z)         对齐 = -np.dot (机械爪接近,世界Z轴)

                                                                                                                                                                                              if alignment > vertical_threshold:         if 对齐 > 垂直阈值:

                                                                                                                                                                                                  if scores[i] > best_score:             if 分数[i] > 最佳分数:

                                                                                                                                                                                                      best_score = scores[i]                 最佳分数 = 分数[i]

                                                                                                                                                                                                      best_grasp = g_world                 最佳抓取 = 世界坐标系抓取

                                                                                                                                                                                          return best_grasp, best_score     return 最佳抓取, 最佳分数

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      G.2. Model Ensemble Temperature Details

                                                                                                                                                                                      G.2. 模型集成温度设置详情

                                                                                                                                                                                      In both single and multi-model settings, 9 candidates responses are generated. For single model, we query Gemini-3-Pro 9 times with temperatures 0.1, 0.2, 0.3,..., 0.9. For multi-model, we query Gemini-3-Pro, Claude-Opus-4.5, and GPT-5.2 3 times each with temperatures 0.1, 0.5, and 0.9. 在单模型和多模型设置中，均生成 9 个候选响应。对于单模型，我们以 0.1, 0.2, 0.3, ..., 0.9 的温度对 Gemini-3-Pro 进行 9 次查询。对于多模型，我们分别以 0.1, 0.5 和 0.9 的温度对 Gemini-3-Pro、Claude-Opus-4.5 和 GPT-5.2 各进行 3 次查询。

                                                                                                                                                                                      G.3. Model Ensemble Prompt

                                                                                                                                                                                      G.3. 模型集成提示词

                                                                                                                                                                                      This section contains the prompts the coding agent uses to generate the final solution from the candidates for both the initial generation and subsequent multi-turn attempts. Text inside curly braces "{}" represent fstring placeholders. 本节包含编码智能体用于从候选响应中生成最终解决方案的提示词，涵盖初始生成及后续多轮尝试。花括号 "{}" 内的文本表示 f-string 占位符。

                                                                                                                                                                                      User prompt for both initial and subsequent generations: 初始生成及后续生成的用户提示词：

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Synthesize the best solution. 综合得出最佳解决方案。

                                                                                                                                                                                      <original_task_description>

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                              {original prompt for candidates}         {候选方案的原始提示词}

                                                                                                                                                                                      </original_task_description>

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                          <candidate_solutions>

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                              {candidate generations}         {candidate generations}

                                                                                                                                                                                          </candidate_solutions>

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      System prompt for initial generation: 初始生成的系统提示词：

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      You are synthesizing {# of candidate generations} candidate Python solutions into 你正在将 {# of candidate generations} 个候选 Python 解决方案合成为

                                                                                                                                                                                      one optimal program. 一个最优程序。

                                                                                                                                                                                              SYNTHESIS RULES:         合成规则：

                                                                                                                                                                                      1. Analyze critically and assume no candidate is fully correct

                                                                                                                                                                                      2. 批判性分析，假设没有候选方案是完全正确的

                                                                                                                                                                                                      2. Prefer explicit checks over assumptions                 2. 优先使用显式检查而非假设

                                                                                                                                                                                      1. Combine the best ideas from multiple candidates when appropriate

                                                                                                                                                                                      2. 在适当情况下结合多个候选方案的最佳思路

                                                                                                                                                                                      1. If candidates disagree fundamentally, choose the more robust approach

                                                                                                                                                                                      2. 若候选方案存在根本分歧，选择更稳健的方法

                                                                                                                                                                                                  OUTPUT FORMAT (strict):             输出格式（严格）：

                                                                                                                                                                                          You may include reasoning before the fenced code block.     你可以在代码块前包含推理过程。

                                                                                                                                                                                      Output ONLY ONE fenced code block (python...) containing the complete final 仅输出一个包含完整最终解决方案的封闭代码块（python...）。

                                                                                                                                                                                      solution. 解决方案。

                                                                                                                                                                                      Do NOT include any other code blocks or code snippets outside this single block. 除此单个代码块外，不得包含任何其他代码块或代码片段。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      System prompt for subsequent generations: 后续生成的系统提示词：

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      You are synthesizing {# of generations} candidate responses for a multi-turn robot 你正在为多轮机器人任务合成 {# of generations} 个候选响应

                                                                                                                                                                                      control task. 控制任务。

                                                                                                                                                                                      DECISION ANALYSIS: 决策分析：

                                                                                                                                                                                          - {regenerate_count} candidates voted REGENERATE     - {regenerate_count} 个候选方案投票选择“重新生成”

                                                                                                                                                                                          - {finish_count} candidates voted FINISH     - {finish_count} 个候选方案投票选择“完成”

                                                                                                                                                                                              SYNTHESIS RULES:         综合规则：

                                                                                                                                                                                          1. Analyze critically and assume no candidate is fully correct     1. 批判性分析，假设没有候选方案是完全正确的

                                                                                                                                                                                                  2. Prefer explicit checks over assumptions             2. 优先使用显式检查而非假设

                                                                                                                                                                                          3. Combine the best ideas from multiple candidates when appropriate     3. 在适当情况下结合多个候选方案的最佳思路

                                                                                                                                                                                              4. If candidates disagree fundamentally, choose the more robust approach         4. 若候选方案存在根本分歧，选择更稳健的方法

                                                                                                                                                                                          5. Combine best code ideas from REGENERATE candidates     5. 整合来自“重新生成”候选方案的最佳代码思路

                                                                                                                                                                                          OUTPUT FORMAT (strict):     输出格式（严格）：

                                                                                                                                                                                      • You may include brief reasoning first

                                                                                                                                                                                      • 可先简要说明理由

                                                                                                                                                                                      • Then output "REGENERATE" on its own line followed by exactly ONE fenced code

                                                                                                                                                                                      • 随后单独一行输出“REGENERATE”，紧跟一个代码块，或单独一行输出“FINISH”

                                                                                                                                                                                      block, OR output "FINISH" on its own line 块，或单独一行输出“FINISH”

Therefore, we experimented with a modified multi-turn prompt which incentivizes verification and debugging, however this did not empirically improve success rate. 我们注意到一种失败情况是任务完成验证不准确。因此，我们尝试了一种改进的多轮提示词，旨在激励验证和调试，但实验结果表明这并未提升成功率。

                                                                                                                                                                                              {console_stdout}         {console_stdout}

                                                                                                                                                                                              1. Line-by-line inspect the executed code         1.逐行检查已执行的代码

Cross-check the code's behavior against the console stdout and stderr         2. 根据控制台标准输出（stdout）和标准错误（stderr）交叉检查代码行为

                                                                                                                                                                                              3. Identify explicit, concrete evidence that each required step of the task was         3. 识别出明确、具体的证据，证明任务的每个必要步骤均已完成

                                                                                                                                                                                      completed 已完成

                                                                                                                                                                                              4. Treat missing evidence, implicit assumptions, or partial signals as failure         4. 将缺失的证据、隐含的假设或部分信号视为失败

                                                                                                                                                                                                  1. Identify specific bugs, failures, missing steps, or incorrect assumptions.             1. 识别具体的错误、故障、缺失步骤或错误的假设。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                              2. Explain why each issue prevents task completion, citing evidence from         2. 解释每个问题为何导致任务无法完成，并引用来自

                                                                                                                                                                                      stdout, stderr, or code behavior. 标准输出、标准错误或代码行为。

                                                                                                                                                                                              3. If the same approach has been attempted multiple times without success, you         3. 如果同一方法已多次尝试仍未成功，请你

                                                                                                                                                                                      MUST try a fundamentally different strategy. 必须尝试一种根本不同的策略。

                                                                                                                                                                                              4. Brainstorm multiple strategies to fix or verify these issues in the next         4. 构思多种策略，以便在下一步中修复或验证这些问题

                                                                                                                                                                                      code generation. 代码生成。

                                                                                                                                                                                              5. Synthesize your brainstorming into a single improved Python program that         5. 将你的头脑风暴整合为一个改进后的 Python 程序，

                                                                                                                                                                                      addresses all identified issues and verifiably completes the task. 解决所有已发现的问题并可验证地完成任务。

                                                                                                                                                                                              6. Respond with the single word 'REGENERATE' followed immediately by new         6. 回复单词“REGENERATE”，并紧随其后提供新的

                                                                                                                                                                                      Python code in a fenced code block (python...) Python 代码块（python...）。

                                                                                                                                                                                          If you choose to regenerate code, you must include your reasoning process only     如果你选择重新生成代码，必须仅在代码开头以注释形式
