                                                                                                                                                                                          - What strategies/APIs have already been tried and why they were insufficient     - 已经尝试过哪些策略/API，以及为何它们不足以解决问题

                                                                                                                                                                                          - How your solution effectively addresses the identified issues     - 你的解决方案如何有效解决已发现的问题

                                                                                                                                                                                          To reiterate, you must only respond with EXACTLY ONE of the following:     重申，你必须仅回复以下选项中的“恰好一个”：

                                                                                                                                                                                          - The word 'FINISH' if you decide to stop generating code     - 如果决定停止生成代码，回复单词“FINISH”

                                                                                                                                                                                          - The word 'REGENERATE' followed immediately by new Python code in a SINGLE     - 如果选择重新生成，回复单词“REGENERATE”，并紧随其后提供

                                                                                                                                                                                      fenced code block (python...). 单个代码块（python...）。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      G.5. Model Ensemble Decreases Average Turn Count

                                                                                                                                                                                      G.5. 模型集成降低了平均轮次

                                                                                                                                                                                      We observed that applying a model ensemble for code generations decreases the average turn count. We noticed that M4 tends to retroactively implement bug fixes and API fallbacks, while the model ensemble preemptively anticipates failures beforehand, resulting in more robust code and lower turn count. See Appendix E.2.4 for a case study on retroactive vs preemptive behavior. 我们观察到，将模型集成应用于代码生成可以降低平均轮次。我们注意到 M4 倾向于事后实施错误修复和 API 回退，而模型集成则能预先规避故障，从而生成更稳健的代码并减少轮次。关于事后行为与预先行为的案例研究，请参阅附录 E.2.4。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 23. CaP-Agent0 decreases average turn count compared to M4 图 23. 与 M4 相比，CaP-Agent0 降低了平均轮次

                                                                                                                                                                                      H. Select Case Studies - Full Generated Code

                                                                                                                                                                                      def execute_pose_move(pose_matrix): def execute_pose_move(pose_matrix):

                                                                                                                                                                                      def pick_and_place(obj_mask, target_center, target_top_z, depth, intrinsics, cam_pose): def pick_and_place(obj_mask, target_center, target_top_z, depth, intrinsics, cam_pose):

                                                                                                                                                                                          cam_pose)     cam_pose)

                                                                                                                                                                                      def pick_object(obs, text_prompt, z_offset=0.0): def pick_object(obs, text_prompt, z_offset=0.0):

                                                                                                                                                                                          Standard pick routine:     标准抓取流程：

                                                                                                                                                                                          1. Segment object     1. 分割物体

                                                                                                                                                                                          2. Plan grasp     2. 规划抓取

                                                                                                                                                                                          3. Execute pick trajectory (pre-grasp -> grasp -> close -> lift)     3. 执行抓取轨迹（预抓取 -> 抓取 -> 闭合 -> 抬起）

                                                                                                                                                                                          """

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Get mask with highest score         #获取得分最高的掩码

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Select best top-down grasp         #选择最佳自上而下抓取

                                                                                                                                                                                                          best_idx = np.argmax(grasp_scores)                     best_idx = np.argmax(grasp_scores)

                                                                                                                                                                                              close_gripper()         close_gripper()

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Lift up (20cm)         #抬起（20厘米）

                                                                                                                                                                                              lift_pos = grasp_pos + np.array([0, 0, 0.2])         lift_pos = grasp_pos + np.array([0, 0, 0.2])

                                                                                                                                                                                      f place_at_position(position, height_offset=0.05) : f place_at_position(position, height_offset=0.05) :

                                                                                                                                                                                          Place currently held object at a specific world position.     将当前抓取的物体放置在特定的世界坐标位置。

                                                                                                                                                                                              Target orientation is usually top-down (gripper pointing down).         目标朝向通常为自上而下（夹爪朝下）。

                                                                                                                                                                                              """

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Standard top-down orientation (gripper pointing -z)         #标准的自上而下朝向（夹爪指向-z轴）

                                                                                                                                                                                              #A common quaternion for top-down is pointing down z-axis.         #一种常见的自上而下四元数是指向z轴负方向。

                                                                                                                                                                                          #Let's assume the current grasp orientation is maintained or we define a fixed top     #假设保持当前的抓取朝向，或者定义一个固定的自上而下

                                                                                                                                                                                          -down.     - 朝向。

                                                                                                                                                                                          #For simplicity, we often maintain the orientation we picked with, or reset to a     #为简化起见，我们通常保持抓取时的朝向，或重置为

                                                                                                                                                                                          known neutral top-down.     已知的标准自上而下朝向。

                                                                                                                                                                                      #Here, we will define a fixed top-down orientation [0, 1, 0, 0] (x-axis rotation #在此，我们将定义一个固定的自上而下朝向 [0, 1, 0, 0]（x轴旋转

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                              180 deg) or similar.         180度）或类似值。

                                                                                                                                                                                              #However, to be safe, let's just use the current robot configuration's orientation         #然而，为保险起见，我们直接使用当前机器人配置的朝向

                                                                                                                                                                                              or a hardcoded one.         或硬编码的朝向。

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Often [0, 1, 0, 0] is top down for Panda.         #通常 [0, 1, 0, 0] 是 Panda 机器人的自上而下朝向。

                                                                                                                                                                                              place_quat = np.array([0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 0.0])         place_quat = np.array([0.0, 1.0, 0.0, 0.0])

                                                                                                                                                                                              target_pos = position + np.array([0, 0, height_offset])         target_pos = position + np.array([0, 0, height_offset])

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Move over target (high)         ##移动至目标上方（高）

                                                                                                                                                                                              hover_pos = target_pos + np.array((0, 0, 0.15))         hover_pos = target_pos + np.array((0, 0, 0.15))

                                                                                                                                                                                              joints = solve_ik(hover_pos, place_quat)         joints = solve_ik(hover_pos, place_quat)

                                                                                                                                                                                              move_to_joints(joints)         move_to_joints(joints)

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Move down to place         ##向下移动以放置

                                                                                                                                                                                              joints = solve_ik(target_pos, place_quat)         joints = solve_ik(target_pos, place_quat)

                                                                                                                                                                                              move_to_joints(joints)         move_to_joints(joints)

                                                                                                                                                                                              open_gripper()         open_gripper()

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Move back up         ##向上移回

                                                                                                                                                                                              joints = solve_ik(hover_pos, place_quat)         joints = solve_ik(hover_pos, place_quat)

                                                                                                                                                                                              move_to_joints(joints)         move_to_joints(joints)

                                                                                                                                                                                              obs = get_observation()         obs = get_observation()

                                                                                                                                                                                                  --- Strategy ---             --- --- 策略 ---

                                                                                                                                                                                                  The stack is Green (top) -> Yellow (mid) -> Blue (bottom).             堆叠顺序为：绿色（顶层）-> 黄色（中层）-> 蓝色（底层）。

                                                                                                                                                                                              Goal: Blue on Yellow.         目标：将蓝色方块放置在黄色方块上。

                                                                                                                                                                                              1. Move Green to the side.         1. 将绿色方块移至一侧。

                                                                                                                                                                                              2. Move Yellow to another spot (target base).         2. 将黄色方块移至另一位置（目标基座）。

                                                                                                                                                                                              #3. Pick Blue.         ##3. 抓取蓝色方块。

                                                                                                                                                                                              #4. Place Blue on top of Yellow.         ##4. 将蓝色方块放置在黄色方块上方。

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Defined drop zones relative to the table center or just hardcoded offsets based         ##定义相对于桌面中心的放置区，或仅基于工作空间知识的硬编码偏移量。

                                                                                                                                                                                              on workspace knowledge.         on workspace knowledge.

                                                                                                                                                                                              green_center, __ = get_object_centroid(obs, "green cube")         green_center, __ = get_object_centroid(obs, "green cube")

                                                                                                                                                                                              if green_center is None: return         if green_center is None: return

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Define temporary drop zones relative to the stack         ##定义相对于堆叠位置的临时放置区

                                                                                                                                                                                              drop_zone_green = green_center + np.array([-0.2, 0.0, -green_center[2] + 0.02]) # Z         drop_zone_green = green_center + np.array([-0.2, 0.0, -green_center[2] + 0.02]) # Z

                                                                                                                                                                                              is roughly table height         约为桌面高度

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Drop zone 2 (for yellow): 20 cm to the right (this will be the final destination         ##放置区 2（用于黄色方块）：向右 20 厘米（这将是最终目的地）

                                                                                                                                                                                              for yellow)         （针对黄色）

                                                                                                                                                                                              drop_zone_yellow = green_center + np.array([0.2, 0.0, -green_center[2] + 0.02])         drop_zone_yellow = green_center + np.array([0.2, 0.0, -green_center[2] + 0.02])

                                                                                                                                                                                              #--- Step 1: Remove Green Cube ---         #--- 第一步：移除绿色方块 ---

                                                                                                                                                                                              print ( "Moving Green Cube..." )         print ( "正在移动绿色方块..." )

                                                                                                                                                                                              success = pick_object(obs, "green cube")         success = pick_object(obs, "green cube")

                                                                                                                                                                                              if success:         if success:

                                                                                                                                                                                                      place_at_position(drop_zone_green, height_offset=0.05) # Place on table                 place_at_position(drop_zone_green, height_offset=0.05) # 放置于桌面上

                                                                                                                                                                                              else:         else:

                                                                                                                                                                                              #Refresh observation         #刷新观测数据

                                                                                                                                                                                              obs = get_observation()         obs = get_observation()

                                                                                                                                                                                              #--- Step 2: Move Yellow Cube ---         #--- 第二步：移动黄色方块 ---

                                                                                                                                                                                              print ( "Moving Yellow Cube...")         print ( "正在移动黄色方块...")

                                                                                                                                                                                              later.         later.

                                                                                                                                                                                      H.3. Additional Analysis Plots

                                                                                                                                                                                      H.3. 补充分析图表

                                                                                                                                                                                      We perform additional quantitative analysis on the cube stack task to understand the impact of multi-turn on success rate. We focus our analysis on Gemini 3 Pro (Google DeepMind, 2025), GPT 5.2 (OpenAI, 2025b), and Claude Opus 4.5 (Anthropic, 2025b), the three strongest performers on CaP-Bench. In particular, we plot the probability density function (PDF) of success over turns (Figure 24), PDF of success over tokens (Figure 25), multi-turn success rate vs turn for the cube stacking task in Figure 26. We find that for the cube stacking task, these models would perform the task on the first try, and use the subsequent turns for recovery. Successes for GPT 5.2 and Claude Opus 4.5 seem to have shorter code length than that of Gemini 3 Pro. 我们对立方体堆叠任务进行了额外的定量分析，以了解多轮对话对成功率的影响。分析重点关注 CaP-Bench 上表现最强的三个模型：Gemini 3 Pro (Google DeepMind, 2025)、GPT 5.2 (OpenAI, 2025b) 和 Claude Opus 4.5 (Anthropic, 2025b)。具体而言，我们绘制了成功率随轮次变化的概率密度函数 (PDF)（图 24）、成功率随 Token 变化的 PDF（图 25），以及立方体堆叠任务中多轮成功率与轮次的关系图（图 26）。我们发现，对于立方体堆叠任务，这些模型通常在第一次尝试时就能完成任务，并将后续轮次用于纠错。GPT 5.2 和 Claude Opus 4.5 的成功代码长度似乎比 Gemini 3 Pro 更短。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 24. Distribution of multi-turn cube stack successes over turns. Results are averaged across M1, M2, and M3. 图 24. 多轮立方体堆叠成功率随轮次的分布。结果为 M1、M2 和 M3 的平均值。

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 25. Distribution of cube stack successes (S1) over tokens 图 25. 立方体堆叠成功率 (S1) 随 Token 的分布

                                                                                                                                                                                       

                                                                                                                                                                                      Figure 26. Cube stack multi-turn success rate vs. turns. Trials with too few or too many turns have lower success rate. Results are averaged across M1, M2, and M3. 图 26. 立方体堆叠多轮成功率与轮次的关系。轮次过少或过多的试验成功率较低。结果为 M1、M2 和 M3 的平均值。

                                                                                                                                                                                      I. LIBERO-PRO Evaluation Results

                                                                                                                                                                                      I. LIBERO-PRO 评估结果

                                                                                                                                                                                      We present detailed task-wise performance of OpenVLA, π0,π0.5 ,and CaP-Agent0 on LIBERO-PRO,which evaluates model generalization under initial position perturbations (Pos) and instruction perturbations (Task). Results are summarized in Table 6, Table 7 and Table 8. Each task was executed over 50 trials. In these tasks, CaP-Agent0 struggles with failures in perception, grasp generation, control APIs. For example, queries of "alphabet soup can" to SAM 3 often results in segmentations of the "tomato sauce can" also present in the scene. Also due to the occluded nature of these scenes and the camera not being top down, many grasps generated on desired objects will be at an angle, this, when combined with the lack of collision-aware motion planning often results in other objects in the scene being knocked over during execution, preventing a secure grasp on the desired object. 我们展示了 OpenVLA、π0,π0.5 和 CaP-Agent0 在 LIBERO-PRO 上的详细任务表现，该基准评估了模型在初始位置扰动 (Pos) 和指令扰动 (Task) 下的泛化能力。结果汇总于表 6、表 7 和表 8 中。每项任务均进行了 50 次试验。在这些任务中，CaP-Agent0 在感知、抓取生成和控制 API 方面存在困难。例如，向 SAM 3 查询“字母汤罐头”时，往往会将场景中同时存在的“番茄酱罐头”也一并分割。此外，由于场景存在遮挡且摄像机并非俯视视角，生成的许多目标物体抓取角度倾斜；当结合缺乏碰撞感知的运动规划时，执行过程中常会导致场景中的其他物体被撞倒，从而无法稳固地抓取目标物体。
